# Awesome Neovim [![Awesome](https://cdn.rawgit.com/sindresorhus/awesome/d7305f38d29fed78fa85652e3a63e154dd8e8829/media/badge.svg)](https://github.com/sindresorhus/awesome)


<img src="https://neovim.io/logos/neovim-mark-flat.png" align="right" width="144" />
<!-- Uncomment the awesome badge when the repository is added to awesome main list.
[![Awesome](https://awesome.re/badge-flat.svg)](https://awesome.re)
-->

> Collections of awesome Neovim plugins. Mostly targeting Neovim specific features. This means Vim-compatible plugins are not listed here.

[Neovim](https://neovim.io/) is a Vim-based text editor engineered for extensibility and usability, to encourage new applications and contributions.

## Plugin Manager

* [lewis6991/pckr.nvim](https://github.com/lewis6991/pckr.nvim) - Spiritual successor of `wbthomason/packer.nvim`.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lewis6991/pckr.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/lewis6991/pckr.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/lewis6991/pckr.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [savq/paq-nvim](https://github.com/savq/paq-nvim) - Neovim package manager written in Lua.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/savq/paq-nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/savq/paq-nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/savq/paq-nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [folke/lazy.nvim](https://github.com/folke/lazy.nvim) - A modern plugin manager, featuring a graphical interface, async execution, a lockfile and more.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/folke/lazy.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/folke/lazy.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/folke/lazy.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [roobert/activate.nvim](https://github.com/roobert/activate.nvim) - A plugin installation system designed to complement `folke/lazy.nvim`.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/roobert/activate.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/roobert/activate.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/roobert/activate.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [nvim-neorocks/rocks.nvim](https://github.com/nvim-neorocks/rocks.nvim) - A modern approach to plugin management using Luarocks, inspired by Cargo.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nvim-neorocks/rocks.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/nvim-neorocks/rocks.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/nvim-neorocks/rocks.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
- [echasnovski/mini.nvim#mini.deps](https://github.com/echasnovski/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-deps.md) - Module of `mini.nvim` for managing other plugins. Uses Git and built-in packages to install, update, clean, and snapshot plugins.

## LSP

### (requires Neovim 0.5)

* [neovim/nvim-lspconfig](https://github.com/neovim/nvim-lspconfig) - Quickstart configurations for the LSP client.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/neovim/nvim-lspconfig.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/neovim/nvim-lspconfig.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/neovim/nvim-lspconfig.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [nvimdev/lspsaga.nvim](https://github.com/nvimdev/lspsaga.nvim) - A light-weight LSP plugin based on Neovim's built-in LSP with a highly performant UI.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nvimdev/lspsaga.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/nvimdev/lspsaga.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/nvimdev/lspsaga.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [kosayoda/nvim-lightbulb](https://github.com/kosayoda/nvim-lightbulb) - The plugin shows a lightbulb in the sign column whenever a `textDocument/codeAction` is available at the current cursor position.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kosayoda/nvim-lightbulb.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/kosayoda/nvim-lightbulb.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/kosayoda/nvim-lightbulb.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [onsails/lspkind.nvim](https://github.com/onsails/lspkind.nvim) - The plugin adds vscode-like icons to Neovim LSP completions.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/onsails/lspkind.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/onsails/lspkind.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/onsails/lspkind.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [ojroques/nvim-lspfuzzy](https://github.com/ojroques/nvim-lspfuzzy) - A small plugin to make the LSP client use FZF.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ojroques/nvim-lspfuzzy.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/ojroques/nvim-lspfuzzy.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/ojroques/nvim-lspfuzzy.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [ray-x/lsp_signature.nvim](https://github.com/ray-x/lsp_signature.nvim) - LSP signature hint when you type.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ray-x/lsp_signature.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/ray-x/lsp_signature.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/ray-x/lsp_signature.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [smjonas/inc-rename.nvim](https://github.com/smjonas/inc-rename.nvim) - Provides an incremental LSP rename command based on Neovim's command-preview feature.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/smjonas/inc-rename.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/smjonas/inc-rename.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/smjonas/inc-rename.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [rmagatti/goto-preview](https://github.com/rmagatti/goto-preview) - Previewing native LSP's goto definition calls in floating windows.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rmagatti/goto-preview.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/rmagatti/goto-preview.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/rmagatti/goto-preview.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [marilari88/twoslash-queries.nvim](https://github.com/marilari88/twoslash-queries.nvim) - Provide inline virtual text displaying TypeScript types for the inspected variables.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/marilari88/twoslash-queries.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/marilari88/twoslash-queries.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/marilari88/twoslash-queries.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [ray-x/navigator.lua](https://github.com/ray-x/navigator.lua) - Learn existing code quickly and navigate code like a breeze. A swiss army knife makes exploring LSP and Tree-sitter symbols a piece of cake.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ray-x/navigator.lua.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/ray-x/navigator.lua.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/ray-x/navigator.lua.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [hedyhli/outline.nvim](https://github.com/hedyhli/outline.nvim) - A significantly enhanced and refactored fork of `symbols-outline.nvim`.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hedyhli/outline.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/hedyhli/outline.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/hedyhli/outline.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [stevearc/aerial.nvim](https://github.com/stevearc/aerial.nvim) - A code outline window for skimming and quick navigation.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/stevearc/aerial.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/stevearc/aerial.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/stevearc/aerial.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [SmiteshP/nvim-navbuddy](https://github.com/SmiteshP/nvim-navbuddy) - A simple popup display that provides breadcrumbs like navigation features using LSP.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/SmiteshP/nvim-navbuddy.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/SmiteshP/nvim-navbuddy.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/SmiteshP/nvim-navbuddy.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [tamago324/nlsp-settings.nvim](https://github.com/tamago324/nlsp-settings.nvim) - Setup LSP with JSON or YAML files.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tamago324/nlsp-settings.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/tamago324/nlsp-settings.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/tamago324/nlsp-settings.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [aznhe21/actions-preview.nvim](https://github.com/aznhe21/actions-preview.nvim) - Fully customizable previewer for LSP code actions.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/aznhe21/actions-preview.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/aznhe21/actions-preview.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/aznhe21/actions-preview.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [mfussenegger/nvim-lint](https://github.com/mfussenegger/nvim-lint) - An asynchronous linter plugin, complementary to the built-in Language Server Protocol support.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mfussenegger/nvim-lint.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/mfussenegger/nvim-lint.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/mfussenegger/nvim-lint.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [b0o/SchemaStore.nvim](https://github.com/b0o/SchemaStore.nvim) - Provide access to the [SchemaStore](https://github.com/SchemaStore/schemastore) catalog.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/b0o/SchemaStore.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/b0o/SchemaStore.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/b0o/SchemaStore.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>

## Completion

* [ms-jpq/coq_nvim](https://github.com/ms-jpq/coq_nvim) - Fast as FUCK Neovim completion. SQLite, concurrent scheduler, hundreds of hours of optimization.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ms-jpq/coq_nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/ms-jpq/coq_nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/ms-jpq/coq_nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [hrsh7th/nvim-cmp](https://github.com/hrsh7th/nvim-cmp) - A completion plugin written in Lua. New version of nvim-compe.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hrsh7th/nvim-cmp.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/hrsh7th/nvim-cmp.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/hrsh7th/nvim-cmp.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [SergioRibera/cmp-dotenv](https://github.com/SergioRibera/cmp-dotenv) - [SergioRibera/cmp-dotenv](https://github.com/SergioRibera/cmp-dotenv)<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/SergioRibera/cmp-dotenv.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/SergioRibera/cmp-dotenv.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/SergioRibera/cmp-dotenv.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
- [echasnovski/mini.nvim#mini.completion](https://github.com/echasnovski/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-completion.md) - Module of `mini.nvim` for asynchronous two-stage completion. Supports showing completion item info and independent function signature.

Supports dot-repeat, different search methods, "last"/"next" extended mappings, Tree-sitter integration, and more.

## Fuzzy Finder

* [nvim-telescope/telescope.nvim](https://github.com/nvim-telescope/telescope.nvim) - Telescope.nvim is a highly [extendable](https://github.com/nvim-telescope/telescope.nvim/wiki/Extensions) fuzzy finder over lists. Built on the latest awesome features from Neovim core. Telescope is centered around modularity, allowing for easy customization.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nvim-telescope/telescope.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/nvim-telescope/telescope.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/nvim-telescope/telescope.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [vijaymarupudi/nvim-fzf](https://github.com/vijaymarupudi/nvim-fzf) - A Lua API for using FZF (Neovim >= 0.5). Allows for full asynchronicity for UI speed and usability.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vijaymarupudi/nvim-fzf.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/vijaymarupudi/nvim-fzf.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/vijaymarupudi/nvim-fzf.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [camspiers/snap](https://github.com/camspiers/snap) - An extensible fuzzy finder. Similar to Telescope, and optimized for performance, especially when grepping in large codebases.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/camspiers/snap.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/camspiers/snap.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/camspiers/snap.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [jvgrootveld/telescope-zoxide](https://github.com/jvgrootveld/telescope-zoxide) - Telescope integration for [zoxide](https://github.com/ajeetdsouza/zoxide), a smart directory picker that tracks your usage.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jvgrootveld/telescope-zoxide.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/jvgrootveld/telescope-zoxide.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/jvgrootveld/telescope-zoxide.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
- [echasnovski/mini.nvim#mini.fuzzy](https://github.com/echasnovski/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-fuzzy.md) - Module of `mini.nvim` with functions to perform fuzzy matching of one string to others along with fast Telescope sorter.
* [axkirillov/easypick.nvim](https://github.com/axkirillov/easypick.nvim) - Easypick lets you easily create Telescope pickers from arbitrary console commands.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/axkirillov/easypick.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/axkirillov/easypick.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/axkirillov/easypick.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [linrongbin16/fzfx.nvim](https://github.com/linrongbin16/fzfx.nvim) - A fuzzy finder that updates on every keystroke.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/linrongbin16/fzfx.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/linrongbin16/fzfx.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/linrongbin16/fzfx.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
- [echasnovski/mini.nvim#mini.pick](https://github.com/echasnovski/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-pick.md) - Module of `mini.nvim` with general purpose interactive non-blocking picker that has one window design, toggleable preview, flexible and fast default match, and much more.
- [echasnovski/mini.nvim#mini.extra](https://github.com/echasnovski/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-extra.md) - Module of `mini.nvim` with extra functionality for its modules. Contains 20+ 'mini.pick' pickers, 'mini.ai' textobjects, and more.

## Colorscheme

### Tree-sitter Supported Colorscheme

Tree-sitter is a new system introduced in Neovim 0.5 that incrementally parses your code into a tree that works, even with errors in your syntax. These colorschemes have specifically set colors for Tree-sitter highlight groups. Vim colorschemes will work with the new groups out of the box.

* [sontungexpt/witch](https://github.com/sontungexpt/witch) - The primary stinvim distro colorscheme includes the default feature of dimming inactive windows, along with various other customization options for users.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sontungexpt/witch.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/sontungexpt/witch.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/sontungexpt/witch.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [Abstract-IDE/Abstract-cs](https://github.com/Abstract-IDE/Abstract-cs) - Colorscheme written in Lua, specially made for roshnivim with Tree-sitter support.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Abstract-IDE/Abstract-cs.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/Abstract-IDE/Abstract-cs.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/Abstract-IDE/Abstract-cs.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [tomasiser/vim-code-dark](https://github.com/tomasiser/vim-code-dark) - A dark color scheme heavily inspired by the look of the Dark+ scheme of Visual Studio Code.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tomasiser/vim-code-dark.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/tomasiser/vim-code-dark.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/tomasiser/vim-code-dark.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [Mofiqul/vscode.nvim](https://github.com/Mofiqul/vscode.nvim) - A Lua port of vim-code-dark colorscheme with vscode light and dark theme.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Mofiqul/vscode.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/Mofiqul/vscode.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/Mofiqul/vscode.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>

### Lua Colorscheme

These colorschemes may not specialize in Tree-sitter directly but are written in Lua.

* [ellisonleao/gruvbox.nvim](https://github.com/ellisonleao/gruvbox.nvim) - Gruvbox community colorscheme Lua port.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ellisonleao/gruvbox.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/ellisonleao/gruvbox.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/ellisonleao/gruvbox.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [metalelf0/jellybeans-nvim](https://github.com/metalelf0/jellybeans-nvim) - A port of jellybeans colorscheme.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/metalelf0/jellybeans-nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/metalelf0/jellybeans-nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/metalelf0/jellybeans-nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [lalitmee/cobalt2.nvim](https://github.com/lalitmee/cobalt2.nvim) - A port of cobalt2 colorscheme using colorbuddy.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lalitmee/cobalt2.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/lalitmee/cobalt2.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/lalitmee/cobalt2.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [calind/selenized.nvim](https://github.com/calind/selenized.nvim) - Lua port of Selenized theme with support for Tree-sitter, nvim-cmp, GitSigns and some more.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/calind/selenized.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/calind/selenized.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/calind/selenized.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>

### Colorscheme Creation

* [tjdevries/colorbuddy.nvim](https://github.com/tjdevries/colorbuddy.nvim) - A colorscheme helper. Written in Lua! Quick & Easy Color Schemes.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tjdevries/colorbuddy.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/tjdevries/colorbuddy.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/tjdevries/colorbuddy.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>

* [ThemerCorp/themer.lua](https://github.com/ThemerCorp/themer.lua) - A simple highlighter plugin for Neovim. It has a huge collection of colorschemes. It also has ability to create colorschemes for Vim/Neovim and other supported apps (such as kitty and alacritty).<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ThemerCorp/themer.lua.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/ThemerCorp/themer.lua.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/ThemerCorp/themer.lua.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
- [echasnovski/mini.nvim#mini.colors](https://github.com/echasnovski/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-colors.md) - Module of `mini.nvim` to tweak and save any color scheme. Also can animate transition and convert between some color spaces.
- [echasnovski/mini.nvim#mini.hues](https://github.com/echasnovski/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-hues.md) - Module of `mini.nvim` to generate configurable color scheme. Takes only background and foreground colors as required arguments. Can adjust number of hues for non-base colors, saturation, accent color, plugin integration.
* [loganswartz/polychrome.nvim](https://github.com/loganswartz/polychrome.nvim) - A colorscheme micro-framework, with support for specifying colors directly in many different formats (sRGB, HSL, Oklab, XYZ and more, with intelligent chroma clipping), live editing preview, and a simple DSL.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/loganswartz/polychrome.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/loganswartz/polychrome.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/loganswartz/polychrome.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>

### Cursorline

* [sontungexpt/stcursorword](https://github.com/sontungexpt/stcursorword) - Highlight the word under the cursor (Improved and compact version of nvim-cursorline).<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sontungexpt/stcursorword.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/sontungexpt/stcursorword.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/sontungexpt/stcursorword.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [RRethy/vim-illuminate](https://github.com/RRethy/vim-illuminate) - Highlight the word under the cursor. Neovim's builtin LSP is available, it can be used to highlight more intelligently.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/RRethy/vim-illuminate.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/RRethy/vim-illuminate.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/RRethy/vim-illuminate.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
- [echasnovski/mini.nvim#mini.cursorword](https://github.com/echasnovski/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-cursorword.md) - Module of `mini.nvim` for automatic highlighting of word under cursor (displayed after customizable delay).
* [mawkler/modicator.nvim](https://github.com/mawkler/modicator.nvim) - Cursor line number mode indicator. Changes the `CursorLineNr` highlight based on Vim mode.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mawkler/modicator.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/mawkler/modicator.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/mawkler/modicator.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>

## Icon

- [echasnovski/mini.nvim#mini.icons](https://github.com/echasnovski/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-icons.md) - Module of `mini.nvim` meant as a general icon provider. Uses fixed set of highlight groups. Supports various categories, icon and style customizations, caching for performance. Integrates with built-in filetype matching.

* [gaborvecsei/usage-tracker.nvim](https://github.com/gaborvecsei/usage-tracker.nvim) - Track your Neovim usage and visualize statistics easily.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gaborvecsei/usage-tracker.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/gaborvecsei/usage-tracker.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/gaborvecsei/usage-tracker.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>

## Terminal Integration

## Dependency Management

* [vuki656/package-info.nvim](https://github.com/vuki656/package-info.nvim) - Display latest package version as virtual text in package.json.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vuki656/package-info.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/vuki656/package-info.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/vuki656/package-info.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [Saecki/crates.nvim](https://github.com/Saecki/crates.nvim) - Rust dependency management for `Cargo.toml`.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Saecki/crates.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/Saecki/crates.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/Saecki/crates.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [piersolenski/telescope-import.nvim](https://github.com/piersolenski/telescope-import.nvim) - Import modules faster based on what you've already imported in your project.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/piersolenski/telescope-import.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/piersolenski/telescope-import.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/piersolenski/telescope-import.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>

## Git

* [f-person/git-blame.nvim](https://github.com/f-person/git-blame.nvim) - Show Git blame info.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/f-person/git-blame.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/f-person/git-blame.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/f-person/git-blame.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [lewis6991/gitsigns.nvim](https://github.com/lewis6991/gitsigns.nvim) - Git integration: signs, hunk actions, blame, etc.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lewis6991/gitsigns.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/lewis6991/gitsigns.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/lewis6991/gitsigns.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
- [echasnovski/mini.nvim#mini.diff](https://github.com/echasnovski/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-diff.md) - Module of `mini.nvim` to interactively visualize difference between buffer text and its reference. Provides toggleable detailed overview in text area, built-in apply/reset/textobject/goto mappings, and more.
- [echasnovski/mini.nvim#mini.git](https://github.com/echasnovski/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-git.md) - Module of `mini.nvim` for enhanced Git integration with current Neovim process. Implements tracking of Git related data, `:Git` user command, and various helpers to explore Git history.
* [NeogitOrg/neogit](https://github.com/NeogitOrg/neogit) - A Magit clone that may change some things to fit the Vim philosophy.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/NeogitOrg/neogit.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/NeogitOrg/neogit.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/NeogitOrg/neogit.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [linrongbin16/gitlinker.nvim](https://github.com/linrongbin16/gitlinker.nvim) - Maintained fork of "ruifm's gitlinker", refactored with bug fixes, ssh aliases, blame support and other improvements.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/linrongbin16/gitlinker.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/linrongbin16/gitlinker.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/linrongbin16/gitlinker.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [tanvirtin/vgit.nvim](https://github.com/tanvirtin/vgit.nvim) - Visual Git Plugin to enhance your Git experience.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tanvirtin/vgit.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/tanvirtin/vgit.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/tanvirtin/vgit.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [sindrets/diffview.nvim](https://github.com/sindrets/diffview.nvim) - Single tabpage interface for easily cycling through diffs for all modified files for any Git rev.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sindrets/diffview.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/sindrets/diffview.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/sindrets/diffview.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [kdheepak/lazygit.nvim](https://github.com/kdheepak/lazygit.nvim) - Plugin for calling lazygit.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kdheepak/lazygit.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/kdheepak/lazygit.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/kdheepak/lazygit.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>

* [aaronhallaert/advanced-git-search.nvim](https://github.com/aaronhallaert/advanced-git-search.nvim) - Search your Git history by commit content, message and author with Telescope.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/aaronhallaert/advanced-git-search.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/aaronhallaert/advanced-git-search.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/aaronhallaert/advanced-git-search.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>

### GitHub

Just edit the issue description.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pwntester/octo.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/pwntester/octo.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/pwntester/octo.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>

## Motion

* [tris203/precognition.nvim](https://github.com/tris203/precognition.nvim) - Precognition uses virtual text and gutter signs to show available motions.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tris203/precognition.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/tris203/precognition.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/tris203/precognition.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [smoka7/hop.nvim](https://github.com/smoka7/hop.nvim) - Hop is an EasyMotion-like plugin allowing you to jump anywhere in a document with as few keystrokes as possible.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/smoka7/hop.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/smoka7/hop.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/smoka7/hop.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [ggandor/lightspeed.nvim](https://github.com/ggandor/lightspeed.nvim) - A Sneak-like plugin offering unparalleled navigation speed via ahead-of-time displayed labels, that eliminate the pause between entering the search pattern and selecting the target.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ggandor/lightspeed.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/ggandor/lightspeed.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/ggandor/lightspeed.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [ggandor/leap.nvim](https://github.com/ggandor/leap.nvim) - A refined successor of Lightspeed, aiming to establish a widely accepted standard interface extension for moving around in Vim-like editors.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ggandor/leap.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/ggandor/leap.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/ggandor/leap.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [ggandor/flit.nvim](https://github.com/ggandor/flit.nvim) - Enhanced f/t motions for Leap.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ggandor/flit.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/ggandor/flit.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/ggandor/flit.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [ggandor/leap-spooky.nvim](https://github.com/ggandor/leap-spooky.nvim) - Spooky (Leap) actions at a distance.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ggandor/leap-spooky.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/ggandor/leap-spooky.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/ggandor/leap-spooky.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [rasulomaroff/telepath.nvim](https://github.com/rasulomaroff/telepath.nvim) - Another Leap extension for performing remote actions with a different approach.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rasulomaroff/telepath.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/rasulomaroff/telepath.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/rasulomaroff/telepath.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [folke/flash.nvim](https://github.com/folke/flash.nvim) - Navigate your code with search labels, enhanced character motions and Tree-sitter integration.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/folke/flash.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/folke/flash.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/folke/flash.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
- [echasnovski/mini.nvim#mini.jump](https://github.com/echasnovski/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-jump.md) - Module of `mini.nvim` for smarter jumping to a single character.
- [echasnovski/mini.nvim#mini.jump2d](https://github.com/echasnovski/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-jump2d.md) - Module of `mini.nvim` for smarter jumping within visible lines via iterative label filtering. Supports custom jump targets (spots), labels, hooks, allowed windows and lines, and more.
* [rlane/pounce.nvim](https://github.com/rlane/pounce.nvim) - An EasyMotion-like plugin for quick cursor movement using fuzzy search.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rlane/pounce.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/rlane/pounce.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/rlane/pounce.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>

* [gen740/SmoothCursor.nvim](https://github.com/gen740/SmoothCursor.nvim) - Add fancy sub-cursor to signcolumn to show your scroll or jump direction.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gen740/SmoothCursor.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/gen740/SmoothCursor.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/gen740/SmoothCursor.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [abecodes/tabout.nvim](https://github.com/abecodes/tabout.nvim) - Jump out of brackets, quotes, objects, etc.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/abecodes/tabout.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/abecodes/tabout.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/abecodes/tabout.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>

* [liangxianzhe/nap.nvim](https://github.com/liangxianzhe/nap.nvim) - Jump between next/previous buffer, tab, diagnostic, etc, with a single key.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/liangxianzhe/nap.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/liangxianzhe/nap.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/liangxianzhe/nap.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>

Considers camelCase and skips insignificant punctuation.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/chrisgrieser/nvim-spider.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/chrisgrieser/nvim-spider.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/chrisgrieser/nvim-spider.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>

## Keybinding

* [folke/which-key.nvim](https://github.com/folke/which-key.nvim) - Neovim plugin that shows a popup with possible keybindings of the command you started typing.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/folke/which-key.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/folke/which-key.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/folke/which-key.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
- [echasnovski/mini.nvim#mini.clue](https://github.com/echasnovski/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-clue.md) - Module of `mini.nvim` to show next key clues. Has opt-in triggers, shows next key information after customizable delay, allows hydra-like submodes, and more.
* [mrjones2014/legendary.nvim](https://github.com/mrjones2014/legendary.nvim) - Define your keymaps, commands, and autocommands as simple Lua tables, and create a legend for them at the same time (like VS Code's Command Palette), integrates with `which-key.nvim`.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mrjones2014/legendary.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/mrjones2014/legendary.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/mrjones2014/legendary.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [slugbyte/unruly-worker.nvim](https://github.com/slugbyte/unruly-worker.nvim) - A ridiculously fun alternative keymap for the workman keyboard layout, with lots of powerful features for working with yank, marks, macros, LSP, and more. Built and configured with Lua.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/slugbyte/unruly-worker.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/slugbyte/unruly-worker.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/slugbyte/unruly-worker.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [FeiyouG/commander.nvim](https://github.com/FeiyouG/commander.nvim) - Create and manage keybindings and commands in a more organized manner and search them quickly through Telescope.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/FeiyouG/commander.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/FeiyouG/commander.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/FeiyouG/commander.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>

Maintained fork of anuvyklack/hydra.nvim.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nvimtools/hydra.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/nvimtools/hydra.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/nvimtools/hydra.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>

It enhances some builtin textobjects, creates extensive set of new ones (like `a*`, `a<Space>`, `a?`, and more), and allows user to create their own (via Lua patterns or functions). Supports dot-repeat, different search methods, consecutive application, and more.

### Indent

Supports customization of debounce delay, animation style, and different granularity of options for scope computing algorithm.

## Session

* [CosmicNvim/CosmicNvim](https://github.com/CosmicNvim/CosmicNvim) - CosmicNvim is a lightweight and opinionated Neovim config for web development, specifically designed to provide a COSMIC programming experience!<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/CosmicNvim/CosmicNvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/CosmicNvim/CosmicNvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/CosmicNvim/CosmicNvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [LazyVim/LazyVim](https://github.com/LazyVim/LazyVim) - Full-fledged IDE powered by **lazy.nvim** to make it easy to customize and extend your config.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/LazyVim/LazyVim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/LazyVim/LazyVim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/LazyVim/LazyVim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>

## External

These tools are used externally to Neovim to enhance the experience.

### Version Manager

* [MordechaiHadad/bob](https://github.com/MordechaiHadad/bob) - A cross platform and easy to use Neovim version manager.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/MordechaiHadad/bob.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/MordechaiHadad/bob.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/MordechaiHadad/bob.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>

### Boilerplate

* [ellisonleao/nvim-plugin-template](https://github.com/ellisonleao/nvim-plugin-template) - Another Neovim plugin template, using GitHub's template feature.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ellisonleao/nvim-plugin-template.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/ellisonleao/nvim-plugin-template.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/ellisonleao/nvim-plugin-template.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>

### OS-specific

* [chrisgrieser/alfred-neovim-utilities](https://github.com/chrisgrieser/alfred-neovim-utilities) - Search Neovim plugins and online `:help` via Alfred (macOS).<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/chrisgrieser/alfred-neovim-utilities.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/chrisgrieser/alfred-neovim-utilities.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/chrisgrieser/alfred-neovim-utilities.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [massix/termux.nvim](https://github.com/massix/termux.nvim) - Interact with Termux APIs, useful to gather various information about your Android phone to display in the statusline (e.g. battery level).<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/massix/termux.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/massix/termux.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/massix/termux.nvim.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [m15a/flake-awesome-neovim-plugins](https://github.com/m15a/flake-awesome-neovim-plugins) - Nix flake that provides Awesome Neovim plugins collection as Nix packages.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/m15a/flake-awesome-neovim-plugins.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/m15a/flake-awesome-neovim-plugins.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/m15a/flake-awesome-neovim-plugins.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>

## Wishlist


## UI

Neovim supports a wide variety of UI's.
You can find them listed on the [Neovim wiki](https://github.com/neovim/neovim/wiki/Related-projects#gui)

## Starter Templates

* [tokiory/neovim-boilerplate](https://github.com/tokiory/neovim-boilerplate) - Starter boilerplate for making new configurations.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tokiory/neovim-boilerplate.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/tokiory/neovim-boilerplate.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/tokiory/neovim-boilerplate.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>
* [frans-johansson/lazy-nvim-starter](https://github.com/frans-johansson/lazy-nvim-starter) - Starter boilerplate with lazy plugin manager.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/frans-johansson/lazy-nvim-starter.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/frans-johansson/lazy-nvim-starter.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/frans-johansson/lazy-nvim-starter.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>

## Vim

- [Vimawesome](https://vimawesome.com/) - Showcases various plugins for Vim and has a [Neovim tag](https://vimawesome.com/?q=tag:neovim) for other plugins targeting Neovim.
- [awesome-vim](https://github.com/akrawchyk/awesome-vim#tools) - Short list of Vim plugins and helpful guides.
* [altermo/vim-plugin-list](https://github.com/altermo/vim-plugin-list) - List of Vim and Neovim plugins.<br><div style="display:flex;"><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/altermo/vim-plugin-list.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Repo stars"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/altermo/vim-plugin-list.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Last Commit"></picture><picture><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/created-at/altermo/vim-plugin-list.svg?style=flat-square&color=blue" alt="GitHub Created At"></picture></div>

## Resource

- [Neovimcraft](https://neovimcraft.com) - A site dedicated to searching specific plugins and guides for building plugins in Lua.
- [Dotfyle](https://dotfyle.com) - Dotfyle is a site for sharing and discovering Neovim configs and plugins.
- [NeoLand](https://neoland.dev) - A beautifully crafted website for Neovim resources.
- [Nvim-training]( https://github.com/Weyaaron/nvim-training) - A beginner-friendly tool for training your 'muscle memory' using small, repeatable tasks.
